2015</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">For more information contact:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Doug Gulling, Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer (515) 222-2309</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">WEST BANCORPORATION, INC. ANNOUNCES RECORD SECOND QUARTER NET INCOME AND DECLARES QUARTERLY DIVIDEND.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">West Des Moines, IA - West Bancorporation, Inc. (NASDAQ: WTBA), parent company of West Bank, is pleased to report that second quarter 2015 net income was $5.3 million, or $0.33 per diluted common share.  This is the highest net income ever recorded by the Company for the second quarter of any year.  This compares to second quarter 2014 net income of $4.7 million, or $0.30 per diluted common share.  On July 22, 2015, the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors declared a regular quarterly dividend of $0.16 per common share.  The dividend is payable on August 19, 2015, to stockholders of record on August 5, 2015.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">For the first six months of 2015, net income was $10.4 million, or $0.65 per diluted common share, up from $9.1 million, or $0.57 per diluted common share, for the first six months of 2014.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8220;Our momentum accelerated in the second quarter,&#8221; commented Dave Nelson, President and Chief Executive Officer of West Bancorporation, Inc.  &#8220;This is the fourth consecutive quarter we have had record earnings for each respective quarter.   In addition, our stock price attained a new record high of $20.99 on July 15, 2015, as reported by Nasdaq. &#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Mr. Nelson added, &#8220;We were able to add new customers and generate new revenue without proportionally increasing our costs.  This was a benefit for both stockholders and customers.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Brad Winterbottom, West Bank President, said, &#8220;Loan growth resumed in the second quarter after taking a breather in the first quarter.  Our pipeline of potential new business continues to be strong.  At June 30, 2015, our loans were 13 percent higher than a year ago, and our deposits were 8 percent higher than a year ago.  We look forward to the second half of 2015.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Lynn Rowat, Eastern Iowa Market President, commented, &#8220;We continue to see solid growth in the loan portfolio in our eastern Iowa market, which increased by over 12 percent during the second quarter.  The loan pipeline is strong, and we expect this growth to continue.  The retail side of our operation is making significant strides with our expanded presence in Coralville, and we are pleased with their efforts.&#8221; </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8220;Our strong momentum in the Rochester market continued through the second quarter with local businesses continuing to choose West Bank as their primary bank,&#8221; said Mike Zinser, Rochester Market President.&#160; &#8220;Our loans outstanding increased to over $68 million at the end of the quarter, an increase of 33 percent since December 31, 2014.&#160; We fueled that loan growth in part with local deposits.&#8221;&#160;&#160; Mr. Zinser continued, &#8220;In addition to offering full service business banking, we&#8217;ve added about a dozen Rochester clients to our Trust Department, which is a nice complement to the banking services we are offering for our business customers.&#160; Of course, our community bank board and local team are very excited about the upcoming groundbreaking for our new bank building, which is planned for the third quarter of 2015.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">The Company filed its report on Form 10-Q with the Securities and Exchange Commission this morning.  Please refer to that document for a more in-depth discussion of our results.  The Form 10-Q document is available on the Investor Relations section of West Bank's website at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#0000ff;text-decoration:underline;">www.westbankstrong.com</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">The Company will discuss its results in a conference call scheduled for 2:00 p.m. Central Time today, Friday, July 24, 2015.  The telephone number for the conference call is 888-339-0814.  A recording of the call will be available until August 8, 2015, by dialing 877-344-7529.  The replay passcode is 10058096.</font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sE125359C60D699081336E9696CA8D418"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">About West Bancorporation, Inc. (NASDAQ: WTBA)</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">West Bancorporation, Inc. is headquartered in West Des Moines, Iowa.  Serving Iowans since 1893, West Bank, a wholly-owned subsidiary of West Bancorporation, Inc., is a community bank that focuses on lending, deposit services, and trust services for consumers and small- to medium-sized businesses.  West Bank has eight offices in the Des Moines metropolitan area; one in Iowa City, Iowa; one  in Coralville, Iowa; and one office in Rochester, Minnesota.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Certain statements in this press release, other than purely historical information, including estimates, projections, statements relating to our business plans, objectives and expected operating results, and the assumptions upon which those statements are based, are &#8220;forward-looking statements&#8221; within the meanings of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, Section 27A of the Securities Act of 1933, and Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;Definitions of ratios:</font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:36px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">Return on average assets - annualized net income divided by average assets.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:36px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">Return on average equity - annualized net income divided by average stockholders' equity.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:36px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">Net interest margin - annualized tax-equivalent net interest income divided by average interest-earning assets.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:36px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;padding-left:12px;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;text-indent:-12px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">Efficiency ratio - noninterest expense (excluding other real estate owned expense) divided by noninterest income (excluding net securities gains and gains/losses on disposition of premises and equipment) plus tax-equivalent net interest income.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:36px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">Texas ratio - total nonperforming assets divided by tangible common equity plus the allowance for loan losses.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:36px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">Allowance for loan losses ratio - allowance for loan losses divided by total loans.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:36px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:bottom;">Tangible common equity ratio - common equity less intangible assets divided by tangible assets.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:36px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:36px;font-size:8pt;"><font
